==========================================================================================

HRS 2020 Early Release 2

Note to Users: This codebook is designed to match the distribution dataset. 
Codebook metadata are derived from the data collection instrument.
If you have questions concerning codebook layout or content please bring
them to the attention of the HRS staff at hrsquestions@umich.edu.

Printing recommendation: Set margins (left/right/top/bottom) to .5 inch; print
in portrait orientation using a mono-space 10-point font.

==========================================================================================

Section J: EMPLOYMENT  (Respondent)

RJ005M1                       CURRENT JOB STATUS- 1
         Section: J     Level: Respondent      Type: Numeric    Width: 2   Decimals: 0
         Ref: SecJ.WORKSTATUS.J005MCurrEmpStatus

         Now we're going to ask you some questions about your current employment
         situation.
         
         Are you working now, temporarily laid off, unemployed and looking for work,
         disabled and unable to work, retired, a homemaker, or what?
         
         INSTR: Do not probe but select all that apply
         
         INSTR: If the respondent sometimes engages in casual work, For example, R works
         at the polls during election time, or works some weeks out of the year but is
         not employed at the time of the survey, then the respondent is not employed.
         		
         WEB-ADMINISTERED TEXT:
         Now we're going to ask you some questions about your current employment
         situation.
                 
         Are you working now, temporarily laid off, unemployed and looking for work,
         disabled and  unable to work, retired, a homemaker, or what?
         
         INSTR: Select all that apply.
         
         INSTR: If you sometimes engage in casual work, for example, you work at the
         polls during election time, occasionally do odd jobs, or work some weeks out of
         the year but are not employed at the time of the survey. We do not consider this
         working now.

         .................................................................................
                        -8.  Web non-response
          4684           1.  WORKING NOW
           421           2.  UNEMPLOYED AND LOOKING FOR WORK
           435           3.  TEMPORARILY LAID OFF
          1798           4.  DISABLED
          7141           5.  RETIRED
           827           6.  HOMEMAKER
           281           7.  OTHER (SPECIFY)
            14           8.  (VOL:) ON SICK OR OTHER LEAVE
            11          98.  DK (Don't Know); NA (Not Ascertained)
            15          99.  RF (Refused)
            96       Blank.  INAP (Inapplicable); Partial Interview

RJ612                         WKS WORKED IN LAST 12 MONTHS
         Section: J     Level: Respondent      Type: Numeric    Width: 2   Decimals: 0
         Ref: SecJ.WORKSTATUS.J612_

         Counting paid vacations as weeks of work, how many weeks did you work in the
         last 12 months?
                 
         INSTR: Count paid sick time as work time
                 
         INSTR: 'Weeks worked' for this question could be from R's current job or any
         other job where R worked for pay during the last 12 months
                 
         INSTR: 0-52 weeks
                 
         WEB-ADMINISTERED TEXT:
         Counting paid vacations as weeks of work, how many weeks did you work in the
         last 12 months?
                 
         INSTR: Count paid sick time as work time.
                 
         INSTR: 'Weeks worked' for this question could be from your current job or any
         other job where you worked for pay during the last 12 months.
         
         INSTR: 0-52 weeks
